        mr-issue-page[issueClosed] {
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;
          position: sticky;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }
        mr-issue-details {
          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

            flex-direction: column;

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 0;

          }

        @media (max-width: 840px) {

          }
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<span class="line"><!---->UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/92.0.4515.107 Safari/537.36 Edg/92.0.902.55<!----></span>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></span>



<br>





### Summary



<span class="line"><!---->### Summary<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A use after free vulnerability exists in the Selection API of Blink rendering engine in Google Chrome 92.0.4515.131 (Stable) and 94.0.4597.1 (Canary). A specially-crafted web page can trigger reuse of previously freed memory which can lead to arbitrary code execution. Victim would need to visit a malicious website to trigger this vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->A use after free vulnerability exists in the Selection API of Blink rendering engine in Google Chrome 92.0.4515.131 (Stable) and 94.0.4597.1 (Canary). A specially-crafted web page can trigger reuse of previously freed memory which can lead to arbitrary code execution. Victim would need to visit a malicious website to trigger this vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





### Tested Versions



<span class="line"><!---->### Tested Versions<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Google Chrome 92.0.4515.131 (Stable)   



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome 92.0.4515.131 (Stable)   <!----></span>



<br>





Google Chrome 94.0.4597.1 (Canary)   



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome 94.0.4597.1 (Canary)   <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





### Product URLs



<span class="line"><!---->### Product URLs<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[



<span class="line"><!---->[<!----></span>





https://www.google.com/chrome/](https://www.google.com/chrome/)



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://www.google.com/chrome/](https://www.google.com/chrome/)"><!---->https://www.google.com/chrome/](https://www.google.com/chrome/)<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





### CVSSv3 Score



<span class="line"><!---->### CVSSv3 Score<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





8.3 - CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:L



<span class="line"><!---->8.3 - CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:L<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





### CWE



<span class="line"><!---->### CWE<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CWE-416 - Use After Free



<span class="line"><!---->CWE-416 - Use After Free<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





### Details



<span class="line"><!---->### Details<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Google Chrome is a cross-platform web browser, developed by Google.



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome is a cross-platform web browser, developed by Google.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A use after free vulnerability exists in Selection API in Blink, which is a main DOM parsing and rendering engine used as core of chromium. More specifically, the vulnerability is manifasted in implementation of `setBaseAndExtent` method. 



<span class="line"><!---->A use after free vulnerability exists in Selection API in Blink, which is a main DOM parsing and rendering engine used as core of chromium. More specifically, the vulnerability is manifasted in implementation of `setBaseAndExtent` method. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





While executing the supplied POC, Chromium browser crashes inside `blink::LayoutObject::LayoutObjectBitfields::IsBox()` at line 17. Snippet of this function is as follows:



<span class="line"><!---->While executing the supplied POC, Chromium browser crashes inside `blink::LayoutObject::LayoutObjectBitfields::IsBox()` at line 17. Snippet of this function is as follows:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





     1:  LayoutObjectBitfields(Node* node)



<span class="line"><!---->     1:  LayoutObjectBitfields(Node* node)<!----></span>



<br>





     2:      : self_needs_layout_for_style_(false),



<span class="line"><!---->     2:      : self_needs_layout_for_style_(false),<!----></span>



<br>





     3:        self_needs_layout_for_available_space_(false),



<span class="line"><!---->     3:        self_needs_layout_for_available_space_(false),<!----></span>



<br>





     4:        needs_positioned_movement_layout_(false),



<span class="line"><!---->     4:        needs_positioned_movement_layout_(false),<!----></span>



<br>





     5:        normal_child_needs_layout_(false),



<span class="line"><!---->     5:        normal_child_needs_layout_(false),<!----></span>



<br>





     6:        pos_child_needs_layout_(false),



<span class="line"><!---->     6:        pos_child_needs_layout_(false),<!----></span>



<br>





     7:        needs_simplified_normal_flow_layout_(false),



<span class="line"><!---->     7:        needs_simplified_normal_flow_layout_(false),<!----></span>



<br>





     8:        self_needs_layout_overflow_recalc_(false), {...} background_paint_location_(kBackgroundPaintInGraphicsLayer),



<span class="line"><!---->     8:        self_needs_layout_overflow_recalc_(false), {...} background_paint_location_(kBackgroundPaintInGraphicsLayer),<!----></span>



<br>





     9:        overflow_clip_axes_(kNoOverflowClip) {}



<span class="line"><!---->     9:        overflow_clip_axes_(kNoOverflowClip) {}<!----></span>



<br>





    10:  {...}



<span class="line"><!---->    10:  {...}<!----></span>



<br>





    11:  // This boolean is the cached value of 'float'



<span class="line"><!---->    11:  // This boolean is the cached value of 'float'<!----></span>



<br>





    12:  // (see ComputedStyle::isFloating).



<span class="line"><!---->    12:  // (see ComputedStyle::isFloating).<!----></span>



<br>





    13:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(floating_, Floating);



<span class="line"><!---->    13:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(floating_, Floating);<!----></span>



<br>





    14:  



<span class="line"><!---->    14:  <!----></span>



<br>





    15:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(is_anonymous_, IsAnonymous);



<span class="line"><!---->    15:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(is_anonymous_, IsAnonymous);<!----></span>



<br>





    16:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(is_text_, IsText);



<span class="line"><!---->    16:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(is_text_, IsText);<!----></span>



<br>





    17:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(is_box_, IsBox);



<span class="line"><!---->    17:  ADD_BOOLEAN_BITFIELD(is_box_, IsBox);<!----></span>



<br>





    18:  {...}



<span class="line"><!---->    18:  {...}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Function that is necessary for triggering vulnerability is "setBaseAndExtent" from "Selection" interface which is responsible for selecting all nodes between two nodes that are provided as arguments to the function. Prototype of this function looks like this:



<span class="line"><!---->Function that is necessary for triggering vulnerability is "setBaseAndExtent" from "Selection" interface which is responsible for selecting all nodes between two nodes that are provided as arguments to the function. Prototype of this function looks like this:<!----></span>



<br>





`setBaseAndExtent(Node anchorNode, unsigned long anchorOffset, Node focusNode, unsigned long focusOffset);`



<span class="line"><!---->`setBaseAndExtent(Node anchorNode, unsigned long anchorOffset, Node focusNode, unsigned long focusOffset);`<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To be able to trigger this vulnerability the provided arguments must have a meaningful hierarchy: anchorNode needs to be parent to the focusNode and parameter anchorOffset must be equal or lower than focusOffset.



<span class="line"><!---->To be able to trigger this vulnerability the provided arguments must have a meaningful hierarchy: anchorNode needs to be parent to the focusNode and parameter anchorOffset must be equal or lower than focusOffset.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>



<br>





At line 4 function UpdateCachedVisibleSelectionIfNeeded is responsible for checking if all nodes are visible. However statement in style element says otherwise because it marks all nodes as "content-visibility: hidden;" which results in engine not properly recognizing visibility of nodes inside "DOMSelection::setBaseAndExtent" function, which finally leads to a use after free vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->At line 4 function UpdateCachedVisibleSelectionIfNeeded is responsible for checking if all nodes are visible. However statement in style element says otherwise because it marks all nodes as "content-visibility: hidden;" which results in engine not properly recognizing visibility of nodes inside "DOMSelection::setBaseAndExtent" function, which finally leads to a use after free vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





With proper manipulation of node elements this vulnerability could lead to control over freed memory and can ultimately result in remote code execution.



<span class="line"><!---->With proper manipulation of node elements this vulnerability could lead to control over freed memory and can ultimately result in remote code execution.<!----></span>

It's hard for me to trace through the whole selection code here, so I'm hoping to get some help :)



<span class="line"><!---->It's hard for me to trace through the whole selection code here, so I'm hoping to get some help :)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The underlying issue seems to be that content-visibility: hidden elements are not updated until it's too late in the stack. Note that we can't simply skip them since I believe that content-visibility: auto, which should still participate in selection, would have the same problem.



<span class="line"><!---->The underlying issue seems to be that content-visibility: hidden elements are not updated until it's too late in the stack. Note that we can't simply skip them since I believe that content-visibility: auto, which should still participate in selection, would have the same problem.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In FrameSelection::ComputeVisibleSelectionInDOMTreeDeprecated(), we update style and layout tree for the document. Much deeper in the stack, in HTMLMeterElement::CanContainRangeEndPoint(), we call UpdateStyleAndLayoutTreeForNode, which forces any ancestor display locks and does the update again. This causes the DCHECK that yosin@ saw, and possibly other issues reported here.



<span class="line"><!---->In FrameSelection::ComputeVisibleSelectionInDOMTreeDeprecated(), we update style and layout tree for the document. Much deeper in the stack, in HTMLMeterElement::CanContainRangeEndPoint(), we call UpdateStyleAndLayoutTreeForNode, which forces any ancestor display locks and does the update again. This causes the DCHECK that yosin@ saw, and possibly other issues reported here.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Ideally, what we want is to gather all DOM nodes that participate in this selection in FrameSelection::ComputeVisibleSelectionInDOMTreeDeprecated(), force them to unlock by DisplayLockUtilities::ScopedForcedUpdate, and then call UpdateStyleAndLayoutTree for the document.



<span class="line"><!---->Ideally, what we want is to gather all DOM nodes that participate in this selection in FrameSelection::ComputeVisibleSelectionInDOMTreeDeprecated(), force them to unlock by DisplayLockUtilities::ScopedForcedUpdate, and then call UpdateStyleAndLayoutTree for the document.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The part that I am not familiar with is how, if possible, to get all of the DOM nodes that participate in this selection. There's a selection_editor_ that is available, which may contain this information. 



<span class="line"><!---->The part that I am not familiar with is how, if possible, to get all of the DOM nodes that participate in this selection. There's a selection_editor_ that is available, which may contain this information. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





yosin@, do you by any chance know how to gather all of these nodes? Or do you know someone who can answer this?



<span class="line"><!---->yosin@, do you by any chance know how to gather all of these nodes? Or do you know someone who can answer this?<!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/484bc1abffcdee33648695244c86daca15ab6539"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/484bc1abffcdee33648695244c86daca15ab6539<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





484bc1abffcdee33648695244c86daca15ab6539



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/484bc1abffcdee33648695244c86daca15ab6539"><!---->484bc1abffcdee33648695244c86daca15ab6539<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Vladimir Levin <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Vladimir Levin &lt;<!----></span>





vmpstr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/vmpstr@chromium.org"><!---->vmpstr@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Tue Aug 24 05:19:07 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue Aug 24 05:19:07 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.



<span class="line"><!---->content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and



<span class="line"><!---->Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and<!----></span>



<br>





layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes



<span class="line"><!---->layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes<!----></span>



<br>





and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.



<span class="line"><!---->and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead



<span class="line"><!---->That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead<!----></span>



<br>





we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.



<span class="line"><!---->we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





R=



<span class="line"><!---->R=<!----></span>





chrishtr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/chrishtr@chromium.org"><!---->chrishtr@chromium.org<!----></a>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2e2f1a09b9ea955912194c4dd4610b00b873efa4"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2e2f1a09b9ea955912194c4dd4610b00b873efa4<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





2e2f1a09b9ea955912194c4dd4610b00b873efa4



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/2e2f1a09b9ea955912194c4dd4610b00b873efa4"><!---->2e2f1a09b9ea955912194c4dd4610b00b873efa4<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Vladimir Levin <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Vladimir Levin &lt;<!----></span>





vmpstr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/vmpstr@chromium.org"><!---->vmpstr@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Wed Aug 25 20:50:40 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Aug 25 20:50:40 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.



<span class="line"><!---->content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and



<span class="line"><!---->Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and<!----></span>



<br>





layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes



<span class="line"><!---->layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes<!----></span>



<br>





and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.



<span class="line"><!---->and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead



<span class="line"><!---->That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead<!----></span>



<br>





we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.



<span class="line"><!---->we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





R=​



<span class="line"><!---->R=​<!----></span>





chrishtr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/chrishtr@chromium.org"><!---->chrishtr@chromium.org<!----></a>





, 



<span class="line"><!---->, <!----></span>





yosin@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/yosin@chromium.org"><!---->yosin@chromium.org<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->(cherry picked from commit <!----></span>

)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

<span class="line"><!---->The following revision refers to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>





  



<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6bf424362b615b227edf1d564555663b24bbccaf



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6bf424362b615b227edf1d564555663b24bbccaf"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6bf424362b615b227edf1d564555663b24bbccaf<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





6bf424362b615b227edf1d564555663b24bbccaf



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/6bf424362b615b227edf1d564555663b24bbccaf"><!---->6bf424362b615b227edf1d564555663b24bbccaf<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Vladimir Levin <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Vladimir Levin &lt;<!----></span>





vmpstr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/vmpstr@chromium.org"><!---->vmpstr@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Tue Sep 07 21:21:46 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue Sep 07 21:21:46 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.



<span class="line"><!---->content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and



<span class="line"><!---->Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and<!----></span>



<br>





layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes



<span class="line"><!---->layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes<!----></span>



<br>





and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.



<span class="line"><!---->and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead



<span class="line"><!---->That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead<!----></span>



<br>





we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.



<span class="line"><!---->we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





R=​



<span class="line"><!---->R=​<!----></span>





chrishtr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/chrishtr@chromium.org"><!---->chrishtr@chromium.org<!----></a>





, 



<span class="line"><!---->, <!----></span>





yosin@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/yosin@chromium.org"><!---->yosin@chromium.org<!----></a>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->(cherry picked from commit <!----></span>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





9723e3c13c8c3e72e0dfeacef00abc97e4a9e3b7



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/9723e3c13c8c3e72e0dfeacef00abc97e4a9e3b7"><!---->9723e3c13c8c3e72e0dfeacef00abc97e4a9e3b7<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Vladimir Levin <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Vladimir Levin &lt;<!----></span>





vmpstr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/vmpstr@chromium.org"><!---->vmpstr@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Tue Sep 07 21:32:03 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue Sep 07 21:32:03 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.



<span class="line"><!---->content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and



<span class="line"><!---->Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and<!----></span>



<br>





layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes



<span class="line"><!---->layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes<!----></span>



<br>





and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.



<span class="line"><!---->and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead



<span class="line"><!---->That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead<!----></span>



<br>





we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.



<span class="line"><!---->we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





R=​



<span class="line"><!---->R=​<!----></span>





chrishtr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/chrishtr@chromium.org"><!---->chrishtr@chromium.org<!----></a>





, 



<span class="line"><!---->, <!----></span>





yosin@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/yosin@chromium.org"><!---->yosin@chromium.org<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





11ff9feda46c2d569bbf84f0e0614ed31e7a1df9



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/11ff9feda46c2d569bbf84f0e0614ed31e7a1df9"><!---->11ff9feda46c2d569bbf84f0e0614ed31e7a1df9<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Vladimir Levin <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Vladimir Levin &lt;<!----></span>





vmpstr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/vmpstr@chromium.org"><!---->vmpstr@chromium.org<!----></a>

<br>





Date: Wed Sep 29 08:26:47 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Sep 29 08:26:47 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[M90-LTS] content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.



<span class="line"><!---->[M90-LTS] content-visibility: Force range base/extent when computing visual selection.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and



<span class="line"><!---->Some of the code that does visual selection ends up updating style and<!----></span>



<br>





layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes



<span class="line"><!---->layout for node. This means that it will temporarily unlock c-v nodes<!----></span>



<br>





and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.



<span class="line"><!---->and may cause a state rewind from layout clean to visual update pending.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead



<span class="line"><!---->That's not an operation we support, verified by DCHECKs. So, instead<!----></span>



<br>





we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.



<span class="line"><!---->we should unlock any c-v nodes prior to getting to layout clean.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





R=



<span class="line"><!---->R=<!----></span>





chrishtr@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/chrishtr@chromium.org"><!---->chrishtr@chromium.org<!----></a>





, 



<span class="line"><!---->, <!----></span>





yosin@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/yosin@chromium.org"><!---->yosin@chromium.org<!----></a>
